## 8. Risks and Dependencies

### 8.1 Technical Risks
- Data synchronization conflicts (offline-first architecture)
- Push notification delivery failure
- Third-party API dependencies (Bible API, meeting finder, payment processors)
- Scalability under rapid growth

### 8.2 Product & User Experience Risks
- Low retention after relapse (compassionate messaging, re-engagement campaigns)
- Privacy concerns deterring adoption (transparent policy, granular controls, security audits)
- Feature overload / complexity (iterative rollout, progressive disclosure, "Simple Mode")
- Insufficient Christian content depth (theological advisory board, partnerships)
- Chatbot providing harmful advice (guardrails, crisis detection, human review, disclaimers)

### 8.3 Business & Market Risks
- Insufficient user acquisition (multi-channel strategy, partnerships, free tier)
- Low premium conversion (clear value proposition, free trial, upsell prompts)
- Competitive threats (unique value proposition, community focus, continuous innovation)
- Regulatory/legal challenges (health tech attorney, compliance from day one)
- Negative press / public controversy (crisis communication plan, security measures)

### 8.4 Organizational & Resource Risks
- Insufficient development resources (iterative development, Flutter single codebase)
- Key personnel turnover (documentation, cross-training, succession planning)
- Insufficient funding (conservative projections, milestone-based fundraising)
- Content creation bottleneck (content calendar, partnerships, AI-assisted drafting)
- Partnership dependency (formal agreements, diversified partnerships, proprietary content)

### 8.5 Dependencies
- AWS (Lambda, DynamoDB, S3, CloudFront, Cognito, SES, SQS/SNS)
- Mobile App Stores (Apple, Google)
- Payment Processors (Stripe, Apple/Google In-App Purchase)
- Push Notification Services (APNS, FCM)
- Bible Content API
- Meeting Finder APIs
- AI/LLM Provider (for chatbot)
- Content Partners
- Flutter (development framework)
- Analytics Platform

---

## 9. Development Roadmap

### 9.1 Full Feature Set

All features listed in Section 4, including bilingual support (English/Spanish), counselor/therapist profiles and content publishing, and all activities, tools, and community features.

**Success Criteria:**
- 25,000 registered users
- 8% premium conversion rate
- 15% Day-90 retention
- $50,000 MRR
- 4.0+ app store rating
- <1% crash rate

---

## 10. Technical Architecture (High-Level)

### 10.1 System Architecture

Decoupled serverless architecture on AWS with Flutter clients (iOS, Android, Web), API Gateway + Cognito, Lambda functions (Go), DynamoDB, SQS/SNS event bus, and third-party integrations.

### 10.2 Technology Stack

| Layer | Technology | Rationale |
|---|---|---|
| Mobile | Flutter (Dart) | Single codebase for iOS, Android, and web |
| Backend Language | Go (preferred), Node.js (acceptable) | Fast Lambda cold starts, strong concurrency |
| Compute | AWS Lambda | Serverless, pay-per-invocation, auto-scaling |
| API Gateway | AWS HTTP API | Native Lambda integration, built-in Cognito authorizer |
| Authentication | AWS Cognito | 50K MAU free tier, OAuth 2.0, social sign-in |
| Database | DynamoDB (on-demand) | Serverless NoSQL, single-digit ms latency |
| Cache | DynamoDB Accelerator (DAX) | Microsecond read latency for hot data |
| Object Storage | AWS S3 | Media, backups, static assets |
| CDN | CloudFront | Edge caching |
| Email | AWS SES | Transactional and notification emails |
| Push Notifications | SNS → APNS / FCM | Fan-out to Apple and Google push services |
| Async Messaging | SQS + SNS | Event-driven architecture |
| Secrets | SSM Parameter Store | API keys, config values |
| Monitoring | CloudWatch + X-Ray | Logs, metrics, alarms, tracing |
| CI/CD | GitHub Actions | Deploys via AWS SAM or CDK |
| IaC | AWS CDK (TypeScript) or SAM | All infrastructure as code |

**Local Development:** LocalStack, Docker Compose, SAM CLI, Flutter hot reload, Makefile/Taskfile

**Estimated Monthly Cost (post-free-tier):** ~$12-38/month

### 10.3 Security & Privacy Architecture

- OAuth 2.0 + JWT tokens (15 min access, rotating refresh)
- RBAC: User, Spouse, Sponsor, Counselor, Admin
- Biometric authentication support
- AES-256 encryption at rest with field-level encryption for critical data
- TLS 1.3 minimum, certificate pinning
- Pre-launch penetration test, annual audit, bug bounty program
- Privacy by Design: data minimization, purpose limitation, user control, right to erasure, no data selling

---

## 11. Conclusion & Next Steps

### 11.1 Summary

Regal Recovery represents a comprehensive, faith-integrated solution for individuals recovering from sex addiction and co-occurring addictions. By combining evidence-based recovery tools with Christian discipleship, robust tracking, AI-powered support, and community accountability, this app addresses the whole person—mentally, intellectually, physically, emotionally, and spiritually.

### 11.2 Immediate Next Steps

1. Stakeholder review and feedback
2. Technical architecture finalization (Flutter, Go/Lambda, DynamoDB, SQS/SNS)
3. Design phase with high-fidelity mockups and user testing
4. Development sprint planning
5. Partnership outreach (SA, AA, Celebrate Recovery, Pure Desire, Bethesda Workshops)
6. Legal & compliance review
7. Content development (affirmations, resources, devotionals — English and Spanish)
8. Development kickoff with CI/CD pipeline

### 11.3 Long-Term Vision

Regal Recovery aspires to become the leading recovery platform for Christians worldwide, expanding beyond sex addiction to support all forms of addiction recovery. Future vision includes global expansion, institutional partnerships, research collaboration, white-label licensing, family healing features, and preventative education.

**Mission:** Empower individuals to experience lasting freedom from addiction through the transforming power of Jesus Christ, supported by cutting-edge technology and compassionate community.
